msg:Across the Hangzhou Bay Bridge...
Also more than 800 rooms! The same afternoon tea (the first Kaiyuan double serving, only chrysanthemum and green tea and only two mini cakes, really mini), the second afternoon tea at a certain hotel in Cixi (self-service, coffee, drinks, snacks, desserts, Infinity...)
There is no difference without comparison.
To be fair, the service of Expo Kaiyuan is still very good, positive and enthusiastic, but the room is rather old-fashioned, and the facilities are also different. The floor where you stay is under renovation (the door card has a card reminder, which can be regarded as normal construction Time, understandable, but with children...). Opposite is the mall! It is convenient to eat, and there is a free umbrella service at the door.
Hope to upgrade the hardware system! I was really unsatisfied with this afternoon tea.
